        <h3 class="yt-lockup-title"><a class="yt-uix-sessionlink yt-uix-tile-link  spf-link  yt-ui-ellipsis yt-ui-ellipsis-2" dir="ltr" title="How To Deal With Anxiety- KAT CHATS #4" data-sessionlink="ei=jfspVKy_OpL1qAXR8YDQBA&amp;ved=CDIQvxs&amp;feature=c4-feed-lik" href="/watch?v=zDLjktRxJK4">How To Deal With Anxiety- KAT CHATS #4</a></h3>
